<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">

    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#userID").val('');
        $("#password").val('');
        $("#userID").focus();
    });

    function validate() {
        var userName = $("#userID").val()
        var password = $("#password").val()
        if (userName == "") {
            $("#userID").focus();
            $("#messageDiv").addClass('collapse')
            updateTips("Please enter LC ID properly.");
            return false;
        }

        if (password == "") {
            $("#password").focus();
            $("#messageDiv").addClass('collapse')
            updateTips("Please enter password properly.");
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }

    function updateTips(msg) {
        $("#validateTips").text(msg).addClass('alert alert-danger alert-dismissable');
    }
</script>
